     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:14px">

     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       1.2      检查范围
      </span>
     </span>
     <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     本次检查仅限于数据库。在这次检查中对数据库配置和数据库性能进行了分析。本报告提供的检查和建议不涉及具体的安全分析和应用程序的具体细节。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     以下提请注意：本次检查仅历时1天，其中还包括了提交分析报告的时间，所以在具体的应用程序性能方面并不加以深入。
    </p>

       存放oracle文件的硬盘区可用空间(oracle文件包括：数据文件，控制文件，在线redo logs，归档redo logs，运行情况文件和跟踪文件)。

     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">

    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     目前该数据库服务器中还没有其他硬盘空间使用率超过90%的分区。如果有需要引起注意并且及时增加硬盘空间的容量。

     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">

       3.3       CPU 利用率
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     CPU利用率的统计时间是：yyyy-mm-dd hh:mi---- yyyy-mm-dd hh:mi
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     1.    top/ glance
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     2.    vmstat2 20
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     参考值：

    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     1.    最大CPU使用率：60%--70%
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     2.    系统进程与用户进程占用CPU最大比率：40/60
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     数据库XXXX:
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     数据库YYYY:
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     从上述的情况中看出，数据库:服务器CPU idle基本在75%以上，CPU资源较为空闲。
     <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     当CPU的使用率超过80%，要注意监控是否有僵死进程，如果有僵死进程占用CPU，需要将僵死进程kill掉。如果有正常进程占用大量CPU，需要查看是否属于正常业务进程等。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>

     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.5       初始化参数文件
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     数据库SPFILE参数指定了当前使用的数据库配置参数，在数据库启动时被使用。在附录A列出了数据库所有的非默认值的参数。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     1.     数据库的参数可以看出大部分都是经过精心设置的。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     2.     建议调整的参数值，请在测试环境数据库中测试确认之后，再调整于生产环境数据库。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.6       CRS日志文件
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     从Oracle 10g RAC版本开始，新增加CRS组件。CRS对于RAC使用是必不可少，因此crs的稳定对于RAC数据库的正常运行至关重要。在健康检查中会检查CRS、CSS和EVM的LOG信息
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     检查CRS其他相关进程日志，没有发现问题。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.7       RDBMS运行日志和跟踪文件
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     Oracle 数据库进程生成跟踪文件来记录错误或冲突，这些跟踪文件可以用来进一步分析问题。数据库参数'max_dump_file_size'限制了这些跟踪文件的大小(以操作系统块的大小为单位)。应当有足够的硬盘空间来容纳最大值的设置，否则的话应当修改上述参数的设置。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     如果参数'max_dump_file_size'设得太大，会超过硬盘空间容量；如果设得太小，又不能容纳足够的出错信息供oracle 支持服务部门分析问题。此参数可以在数据库会话级设置，这样可以有选择性地设置较大值。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     注意每天监控运行日志文件中的出错信息，以便于在问题还是隐患的时候及时发现并解决掉。建议每月初将当前的alert.log重新命名以作备份，同时也可以避免alert.log文件变得太大不易管理。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     在数据库:实例的运行日志文件发现的最近一月内的主要错误如下所示：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     1.……
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     2.……
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.8      控制文件
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     每个数据库至少有一个控制文件。控制文件记录了数据库的物理结构及同步信息。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Control filelocation
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     控制文件路径如下：
    </p>

     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">

        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Name
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)" width="204">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Status
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-left-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-left-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="207">

        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-left-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-left-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="207">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="220">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-left-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-left-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="207">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="220">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>

     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     目前所有的控制文件文件存储在已经做了硬件RAID的磁盘阵列上面，提供了硬件级别的保护。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议 :
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.9      Redolog 文件
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     对于恢复操作，最为关键的结构是在线RedoLog。在线Redo Log一般由两个或两个以上预先分配的存储数据库变化的文件组成。为了防止例程故障，每个数据库的实例都有相关的在线Redo Log。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     每个数据库至少有两个RedoLog组，每组至少有一个日志文件。Oracle的多重在线RedoLog文件可以确保在线日志文件的安全。对于多重在线Redo Log文件，LGWR同时将相同的Redo Log信息写入不同的Redo Log文件中，从而减少单个文件丢失的损失。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     当Oracle无法访问一个Redo Log文件时，这个文件状态变为INVALID。当Oracle推测一个Redo Log文件不完整或者不正确时，它的状态变为STALE。当一个STALE的文件被重用时，即其所在日志文件组活动时，此文件也能够使用。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     在线Redo Log文件减少了数据库数据丢失的损失，比如当发生例程故障时，没有被写入数据文件的数据可以从在线Redo Log文件中恢复。
    </p>
    <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style='margin:0px 0px 10px; padding:0px; border-collapse:collapse; width:668px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Group  #
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Thread  #
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Sequence  #
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Bytes
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Members
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Archived
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Status
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">

         First  Change #
        </p>
       </td>

         First Time

       </td>

    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.10    归档Redo log 文件
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     Oracle允许将写满的在线Redo Log文件存放在一个或多个脱机位置，即归档Redo Log。在线日志文件通过归档写入归档日志文件。后台进程ARCn自动进行归档操作。您能通过归档日志进行：
    </p>
    <ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0px 0px 30px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       在线备份
      </p>
     </li>
     <li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       基于时间的恢复
      </p>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Archived Redo Log Settings
     </span>
    </h5>
    <table cellpadding="0" style='margin:0px 0px 10px; padding:0px; border-collapse:collapse; width:668px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)" width="199">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Parameter
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)" width="238">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Value
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="199">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="238">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="199">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="238">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="199">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="238">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     这里能够很好地在运行环境中使用归档Redo Log。这样就能够进行基于时间的恢复。监控归档日志文件所暂时存放的磁盘空间，根据实际情况调整归档日志文件备份到磁带的频度。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.11    数据文件
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     数据文件是数据库分配的物理文件。在Oracle数据库中，一个表空间可以包含一个或多个物理文件。而一个数据文件则只能关联一个表空间和一个数据库。Oracle通过分配一定的磁盘空间以及所需要的文件头空间，为每个表空间创建一个数据文件。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Data file locations
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     检测数据文件的位置。当数据文件增长过度，数据库中必须添加数据文件。应该避免“哪里有空间，哪里建文件”的错误方法，因为这样会增加备份策略和文件维护的复杂性。下面列出部分数据文件的位置。
    </p>
    <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style='margin:0px 0px 10px; padding:0px; border-collapse:collapse; width:736px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important' width="755">
     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">

    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     目前看来，数据文件存放位置基本准确。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Autoextend capabilities
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     通过自动扩展命令进行数据文件的自动扩展。假定数据文件无法分配所需空间，那么它将提高数据文件的大小以获得更多空间。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.12    表空间
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     每个数据库由一个或多个逻辑存储单位，即表空间，所组成。而表空间则由逻辑存储单位段所组成。而段将被分为多个片。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      TablespaceManagement
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     以下是关于数据库表空间管理的信息。
    </p>
    <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style='margin:0px 0px 10px; padding:0px; border-collapse:collapse; width:668px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important' width="552">
     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Status
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Name
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Type
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Extent Management
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Segment  Space Management
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Size (MB)
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Used  (MB)
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)" width="65">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Used  (%)
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-left-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-left-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">

        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>

       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="65">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>

      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">

       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">

       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">

       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="65">
