      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-left-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-left-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="65">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Tablespace Default Storage Management
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     每个表空间中，可以为创建的对象指定缺省的存储参数。创建对象时指定的存储参数将覆盖缺省值。如果在创建对象时没有指定存储参数，那么系统将使用缺省值。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     表空间缺省存储情况：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     数据库表空间的管理方式均为本地管理，这有利于减少表空间级别的碎片，同时避免了DB在进行空间管理时对数据字典表（FET$、UET$）的争用。我们知道系统中存在越多的空闲extent,越容易发生碎片问题。其中空闲extent的大小非常重要，如果在表空间上有许多个无法满足指定的next大小的空闲extent，那这个空闲extent就无法被重新使用并成为碎片，这时就需要重新整理碎片；我们可以使用COALESCE命令合并相邻的extent，来减少系统中的碎片。如果系统中不连续的小空闲extent过多，也就是碎片过多，则可能需要通过重建表空间的方式来消除碎片。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     系统多数表空间使用ASSM，ASSM使用位图而不是传统的FreeList来管理段内的free db block，大大提升了空间管理的性能。同时显著的减少segmentheader类型的buffer busy wait等待事件。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     表空间的管理方式选择合理。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Next Extent
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     保证段能够增长是很重要的，因此在必要时分配next extent。如果在表空间中没有足够的空余空间，那么next extent无法分配，对象也无法增长。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     在数据库中没有发现无法分配NEXTEXTENT的段。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Temporary Tablespace
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     临时表空间用于存放临时段。为了维护数据库的性能，临时表空间的维护方法有别于其他一般表空间。缺省情况下，所有表空间都创建为PERMANENT。所以在创建临时段时，需要保证表空间类型为TEMPORARY。由于这些表空间中的排序段不被清除，所以减少了空间事务争夺，同时减少了SMON对于CPU的使用率。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     当进行长时间清理时，用户无法进行排序操作。在这种情况下，可以指定用户使用状态为PERMANENT的临时表空间。这有可能会引起空间事务争夺，但是可以允许用户在磁盘上进行排序操作。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     由于表空间的extent 使用了local management 方式，对表空间采用位图管理，更利于空间的使用及回收管理。
    </p>
    <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style='margin:0px 0px 10px; padding:0px; border-collapse:collapse; width:668px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Status
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)" width="59">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Name
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)" width="75">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Size (MiB)
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Minimum Extents
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Maximum Extents
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Minimum Extent Length
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-top-width:1px; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:solid solid solid none; border-top-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Increase (%)
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-left-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-left-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="59">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%" width="75">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border-right-width:1px; border-bottom-width:1px; border-style:none solid solid none; border-right-color:rgb(153,153,102); border-bottom-color:rgb(153,153,102); max-width:100%">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     在数据库TEMP为TEMPORARY类型的表空间，Extent Management 方式为LOCAL。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     保证每一个数据库用户都被分配一个临时类型的TEMP表空间。以下列出了将PERMANENT表空间作为默认临时表空间的用户：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     没有发现用户将PERMANENT表空间作为默认临时表空间。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       4.13    回滚段管理
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     回滚段能够用来保证读一致性，回滚事务以及恢复数据库。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Rollback Segment List
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
    </p>
    <h3 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:20px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       5. 数据库简单风险评估
      </span>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       5.1      安全性管理
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     在安全性方面，主要考虑用户访问数据库的控制以及维护系统的安全性问题。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      Database Administrator Usernames/Passwords
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     Oracle自动生成两个用户，并授予DBA权限：
    </p>
    <ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0px 0px 30px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       SYS
      </p>
     </li>
     <li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       SYSTEM
      </p>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     经检查，SYS和SYSTEM都没有使用初始缺省密码。这样有利于维护数据库的安全性，否则任何具有Oracle知识背景的人都能进入数据库。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     目前数据库用户安全方面设置良好，设置安全合理。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      SYSDBA Users
     </span>
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     被授予SYSDBA权限的用户能够进行DBA的操作，包括建立数据库，关闭数据库。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     目前数据库不存在具有DBA权限的业务用户，用户权限管理情况较好。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
    </p>
    <h3 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:20px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       6.  SqlNet 概况
      </span>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     Net8能够在不同计算机上安装服务和应用程序，并且能够使它们如同同一层上的应用程序一样进行通信。Net8的主要功能就是创建网络通话，并且在客户端和服务器端，或者两个服务器端之间转换数据。Net8必须安装在网络的每台机器上。当网络通路建立，Net8扮演着客户端和服务器端数据投递者的角色。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       6.1       监听器Listener
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     位于服务器端的监听程序是单独的进程。它从客户端接受连接请求，并管理这些对服务端的请求。当前LISTENER的参数设置如下：
    </p>
    <table cellpadding="0" style='margin:0px 0px 10px; padding:0px; border-collapse:collapse; width:668px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)" width="248">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Parameter
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(204,204,153)" width="62">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Value
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="248">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         STARTUP_WAIT_TIME_LISTENER
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="62">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         N/A
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="248">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         CONNECT_TIMEOUT_LISTENER
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="62">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">

        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         TRACE_LEVEL_LISTENER
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(247,247,231)" width="62">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">

    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     只有当SQLNET需要跟踪判断所出现的问题时，TRACE_LEVEL_LISTENER才需要被设置。所获得的跟踪文件需交由OracleSupport进行分析。SQLNET跟踪只需在一段时间内开启，因为这将占用一些网络资源。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>

      <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
       6.3      TNSNAMES
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     TNSNAMES.ORA包含与连接描述符相匹配的网络服务名。连接描述符包括监听程序的地址以及connect_data。TNSNAMES.ORA设置如下：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     由于TNSNAMES中相关的网络服务名比较多，完整的TNSNAMES.ORA中的内容可以见服务器上的配置文件。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>

     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:20px">

     </span>

     数据库的性能情况通过AWR的报告来体现。由于本次检查并不是完整的性能检查，所以本报告只列举最主要的性能问题。

     我们选取业务最为繁忙的上午时段的AWR报告进行分析。

       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="146">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         CPU used by this session
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="68">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="74">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="65">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important" width="146">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         parse time cpu
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important" width="68">

       </td>

        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         recursive cpu usage
        </p>

       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="68">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>

        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="65">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     分析：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     可以看出系统CPU主要用于SQL语句的真正的执行阶段。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     二、关于数据库事务提交/会滚性能指标
    </p>
    <table cellpadding="0" style='margin:0px 0px 10px; padding:0px; border-collapse:collapse; width:668px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important' width="422">
     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">

        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>

        </p>
       </td>

        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">

        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">

        </p>

       </td>

      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">

        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         user rollbacks
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="87">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>

        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="64">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>

     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     分析：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     在实例快照统计中，用户回滚率正常。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       7.6       数据库I/O性能
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     1、本数据库的数据文件绝大部分的平均的读取时间&lt;20ms,表示当前的数据库I/O速度是可以接受的，如果有一些数据文件的平均读取时间大于20ms，需要引起注意。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     2、ORACLE认为平均读取时间大于20ms是I/O性能比较差的，如果一个数据文件的平均读取时间一直大于20ms的话，建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     应该检查对该数据文件上的查询语句，并且优化SQL语句。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     如果该数据文件包含索引，一个可以考虑的选择是使用压缩索引来减少I/O。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     数据文件应该尽量条带化，分布在不同的物理硬盘上面。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       7.7      索引/行迁移/行链
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     索引
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     索引需要维护。对于表的删除或者添加操作都会间接地对索引进行相应操作。过时的索引结构会产生碎片，此时索引需要被重新建立。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     当前数据库中未发现需要重建的索引。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     行链
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     当一条记录太大，一个数据块无法将其存储时，oracle 就会将其存储在相链接的块中。如果一条记录中含有数据类型如：LONG,LONGRAW,LOB,行链则无法避免。
    </p>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     行迁移
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     当一个数据块已满，而一条记录在更新后记录长度增加了，这时oracle 就会将整个记录迁移到一个新的数据块，这就是行迁移。Rowid 在行迁移之后保持不变。除大数据类型之外，上述情况对数据库的性能是有影响的。从上面实例活动统计部分的table fetch continued row分析可以看出当前数据库中链接行的多少。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     关于行迁移/行链接统计信息
    </p>
    <table cellpadding="0" style='margin:0px 0px 10px; padding:0px; border-collapse:collapse; width:668px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important' width="422">
     <tbody style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px 4px 2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(0,102,204)" width="182">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px 4px 2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(0,102,204)" width="80">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         Total
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px 4px 2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(0,102,204)" width="85">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         per Second
        </p>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px 4px 2px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(0,102,204)" width="65">
        <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
         per Trans
        </p>
       </td>
      </tr>
      <tr style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="182">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="80">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="85">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
       <td style="margin:0px; padding:0.1px; word-wrap:break-word!important; word-break:break-all; border:1px solid rgb(221,221,221); max-width:100%; background:rgb(255,255,204)" width="65">
        <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
       </td>
      </tr>
     </tbody>
    </table>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     目前行链接较少，但是仍需关注，是否行链接集中在特定的segment，以及是否属于不可避免的行链接情况。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     为避免或者尽量减少出现行链接/行迁移的可能，建议适当增大表、表分区的pctfree存储参数。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       7.8       Enqueue等待分析
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     在统计报告中的TOP5 event中均没有出现Enqueue等待事件，说明Enqueue等待不是系统的性能瓶颈，性能良好。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
       7.9       Latch分析
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     在数据库的latch命中率为n%以上，符合要求。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">

    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     1、使用explain plan去分析TOP SQL的执行计划，找出消耗资源较高的原因。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>
    </p>
    <h3 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:20px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       8.  数据库备份策略评估
      </span>
     </span>
    </h3>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       8.1       备份
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     备份策略：
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     每天对数据库做全库备份。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议：
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     使用RMAN对数据库进行备份。
    </p>
    <h4 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:18px">
      <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       8.2       恢复
      </span>
     </span>
    </h4>
    <h5 style='margin:0px 0px 15px; padding:0px; font-weight:400; font-size:16px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     恢复策略：
    </h5>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     建议:
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     定期进行恢复测试以确保备份的可用性和恢复步骤的熟悉。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     1、根据不同的数据库失败情况制定相应的恢复策略。
    </p>
    <ul class="list-paddingleft-2" style='margin:0px; padding:0px 0px 0px 30px; max-width:100%; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; line-height:25.6px; widows:1; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       数据库全库恢复
      </p>
     </li>
     <li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">

       数据文件恢复
      </p>
     </li>
     <li style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important">
      <p style="margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important">
       数据表恢复
      </p>
     </li>

    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     2、根据制定的恢复策略进行恢复测试。
    </p>
    <p style='margin-top:0px; margin-bottom:15px; padding-top:0px; padding-bottom:0px; max-width:100%; clear:both; min-height:1em; color:rgb(62,62,62); font-family:"Helvetica Neue",Helvetica,"Hiragino Sans GB","Microsoft YaHei",Arial,sans-serif; font-size:16px; widows:1; line-height:1.75em; word-wrap:break-word!important'>
     <br style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important"/>

     <span style="margin:0px; padding:0px; max-width:100%; word-wrap:break-word!important; font-size:20px">
